<section class='search__header'>
<h1 class='search__header__title'>people Photos</h1>
<p class='search__header__subtitle hide-if-signed-in'>This search page features pictures of people, people photography and portrait pictures. All these free images of people can be used according to the open Pexels license. This is a huge collection of free people stock photos and people photography.</p>
</section>
